I called in to make an appointment for the orthodontist and general dentist. They were able to get me in to see both that very same week! My first experience over the phone with Elisa was really good she helped guide me in what the steps would be to be seen and explained they had payment options which was my biggest concern. Once I went in I was amazed by the appearance it is not your normal dentist office it is very modern. You walk in and it smells great, they have a fridge with waters, then their is coffee, and  you can watch movies or shows in their lobby!

I met Corina who took my xrays and was very sweet and patient since I have a gag reflex and can be pretty difficult to take xrays on. After the xrays I met Valerie & Dr. Singh who explained what treatment I needed, and helped me get in the right step s for the orthodontist.
He is a good looking doctor to ladies! Forget Dr.Mcdreamy , Dr. Singh is the new Mc dreamy lol.

That Friday I saw dr saper for braces which I have been wanting since my 20's but was never able to afford. He explained to me the different options I had for braces to correct by Bite. He is such a smart doctor and is very detailed which I appreciated because I rather know everything then be surprised later.

Sorry for the rant but an office like this deserves it !

I have my next appointment for ortho next month, then my 3 month cleaning in August!!!!< /Review>

<user>117572589810953038564<//user><Name>Steve Clemmons< /Name><date>1580755110720<//date>< Rate>

< Review>
I miss the institution in Oakland. I hate having to come all the way to Napa to experience a true Italian delicatessen. But every time I'm in Napa, this is a must-stop place. The clam chowder is extremely delicious with big pieces of clam. They're friendly and move very quickly to get through the long lines. It is worth the wait. My go-to sandwich is the Italian combo with hot coppa added on an onion roll. Other things of note that I've never leave without are the deviled eggs and the stuffed peppers with prosciutto and feta cheese.<//Review>

<UserId.>112053969133310512879< /UserId.><Name>Shaun Keeler< /Name><Time>1549527111995<//Time>< rating>
5< /rating>
< review>
Great Deli!
Depending on the time of day, parking usually very good. Awesome, and high quality sandwich meats. They also serve hot food for lunch specials. High quality desserts. It's a little expensive, but it's worth the price for good quality food.

When you go in, you need to take a ticket with a number on it. With this in mind, they will call out your number when you're up. This is when you place your order. They also have all types of cold salads, macaroni, ravioli, several types of potato salads.

They also offer imported dry foods, which you can't get at other stores. This is a high end Delicatication. They also offer hot soups. I really do appreciate these types eateriess.< /review>

< review>
I am gluten free, not by choice, and when I asked if the polenta was gluten free, I was rudely dismissed with "We don't have anything gluten free". Well, they have meats, chicken, some salad, etc. When I stated that polenta is usually gf, the man went and asked his co worker and was dismissed as nothing is gf here. I was struck by how arrogant the taller guy was as he asked me if I had a number when I was one of two people standing at the counter. There were no numbers as they were stuck in the machine. He sent me back to the original guy waiting on my sister. There was no friendliness at all as I remember from a few years back. I ordered a couple of slices of roast beef and cheese. I was appalled that the man picked them up with his hands. We should have walked out then and there. He packed it in the bag with the hot soup and lasagna and when I got home, the cheese was melted and stuck to the paper. My mother said the minestrone was not flavorful so was quite disappointed. The arrogance and lack of good customer service is off putting.< /review>
